INSPIRATION TUTORIAL
『靈感』說明=Inspiration
<color\=#FFD145>靈感提升</color>\n{{A}}錄入面具全書後，可以領取靈感點。\n使用靈感點，可以解鎖並提升靈感技能等級。\n\n<color\=#FFD145>靈感重置</color>\n靈感技能可以消耗魂石進行重置。\n重置後返還所有已消耗的靈感點。=<color\=#FFD145>Inspiration</color>\nWith every new Persona recorded in the book, you will earn Inspiration Points, which can be used to unlock and upgrade Wonder's skill tree. More skills and levels are unlocked as you level up further.\n\n<color\=#FFD145>Inspiration Reset</color>\nYou can reset your skill tree by spending Konpaku Gem, which will return all the Inspiration Points you have used.

海濱經營大作戰·稀有事件=Seaside Business Blitz·Rare Events
事件有<color\=#ff3b37>稀有度</color>區分，稀有度越高，事件效果越好。\n處理帶有「<color\=#ff3b37>STORY</color>」標誌的事件時會遇到經營分歧，\n做出不同的決定會獲得不同的經營效果。=Events have different <color\=#ff3b37>rarity</color>, the higher the rarity, the better the effects. Solving events with a [<color\=#ff3b37>STORY</color>] logo will have different branches, making different decisions will lead to different business effects.
遇到了高稀有度的「<color\=#ff3b37>特殊事件</color>」，\n快去前往處理吧！=Encountered a rare [<color\=#ff3b37>Special event</color>],\nlet's go solve it!
遇到了經營分歧，\n不同選擇會影響後續<color\=#ff3b37>經營效果</color>，\n請謹慎做出決策！=You've encountered a business divergence.\nYour choice will impact future <color\=#ff3b37>business effects</color>, \nchoose carefully!
海濱經營大作戰·夥伴體力=Seaside Business Blitz·Companion Stamina
處理部分事件會消耗經營夥伴「<color\=#ff3b37>體力</color>」，\n當體力過低時，處理事件的<color\=#ff3b37>成功率</color>也會相應降低。\n未參與經營的夥伴在經營日結束後會自動恢復體力。=Certain events will cost [<color\=#ff3b37>Stamina</color>].\nWhen Stamina is too low, decrease the <color\=#ff3b37>Success Rate</color> accordingly.\nNon-active Companions will restore all Stamina at the end of business day.

Character's Story
----------
限時關卡中，攜帶指定怪盜可額外獲得一定比例的通關獎勵，同時攜帶多名指定怪盜時，額外比例相加。=In the limited time levels, bringing specific Thieves can increase rewards.

敵方陣容=Foes
關卡描述=Description

At the start of battle, {{A}} will give all Thieves Lifelink, then decrease Thieves' Healing Received by $1. [{{A}}'s Claw]: Deal damage to 1 foe, inflict the target with Laceration: Take Damage Over Time, can be dispelled.\n4. [{{A}}'s Fang]: Deal damage to all foes, inflict all Thieves with Bite: Increase DMG Taken, dispelled after using a buff skill.\n5. At the start of turn, if a target has both Laceration and Bite, automatically use Prey: Deal heavy damage, then inflict the target with Brainwash."
